his moder. & hine his wife ge-þeot. 

& beoð twegen on anen flæsce. witodlice ne 
synden na twegen. ac an flæsc. 

þt god ge-samnode ne syndrige þt nan man. 

And eft innen huse his leorning-cnihtes hine be 
þam ylcen acsoden. 

Ða cwæð he. swa hwilc man swa his wif for-læt 
& oder nymð unriht-hameð he wyrcð þurh hyo. 

Ænd gyf þt wif hire were forlæt & oðerne 
nymð. hyo unriht-hæmeð. 

Ænd hyo brohten him heore litlenges þt he his 
æt-rine. þa cyddan his leorning-cnihtes þam þe 
hyo brohten. 

Ða se hælend hyo ge-seah un-wurðlice he hit 
for-beod & saigde heom. Lateð þa litlinges to me 
cumen & ne for-beode ge heom. soðlice swilcere is 
heofone rice. 

Soðlice ic segge eow swa hwilc swa godes rice ne 
on-fehð swa swa litling ne maig he on þt. 

Ða be-clepte he hyo & his hande ofer hyo settende 
bletsede hyo. 

And þa he on weige eode sum hym to arn & 
ge-begden cneowen to-foren hym cwæð & bæð 
hine. La gode lareow hwæt do ic þæt ic ece lyf 
age. 

Þa cwæð se hælend hwi saigst þu me godne; nis 
nan man god buton god ane. 

Canst þu þa be-bode. ne unriht-hæm þu. ne slyh 
þu. ne stel þu. ne sege þu lease ge-witnysse. 
fæcen ne do þu. wurðe þine fæder & þine 
moder. 

Ða andswerede he gode. lareow eall þis ic heold 
of minre geogeðe. 

Se hælend hine þa behealdende hyfode (sic) & 
saide hym. An þing þe is wane. syle eal þæt 
þu age. & syle hit þearfen þanne hafst þu þt 
goldhord on heofene. & cum & folge me. 

& for þan worde he wæs unge-rot. & ferde 
gneorgende for þan he hæfde mycele ehte. 

Ða cwæð se hælend to hys leorning-cnihten hine 
be-seonde. swiðe earfedlice on godes rice gað 
þa þe feoh hæbbeð. 

Ða forteden his leorning-cnihtes be his worden. 
Eft se hælend heom andswerede & cw. Eala chyld. 
swiðe earfodlice þa þe on hire feo ge-truwiad 
gad on godes rice. 

eaðere is olfende to farene þurh nædle þyrl. 
þanne se rice & se welege on godes rice ga. 

Hyo þas þe ma be-twexe heom wundreden & 
cwæðen. & hwa mæig beon hal. 

þa be-heold se hælend hyo & cwæð. Mid mannen 
hit is un-eaðelic. ac na mid gode. Ealle þing 
mid gode synde eaðelice. 

Þa on-gan petrus cweðen. Witodlice we ealle 
þing for-leten. & folgeden þe. 

Ða andswerede hym se hælend. Nis nan þe his hus 
for-læt. oððe ge-broðre. oððe swuster. 
oððe fæder oððe moder. oððe bearn. oððe 
aceres for me. & for þam godspelle. 

þe hundfeald ne on-fo. nu on þisse tide. hus & 
broðre & swustre. & fæder & moder & bearn. & 
æceres. mid ehtnyssen & on to-wearde wurlde ece 
lyf. 

Manege fyrmeste byð ytemeste. & ytemeste 
fermeste. 

Soðlice hyo ferden on weige to ierusalem. & se 
hælend heom beforen eode. & hyo adreddem heom 
hine. & him felgden. & eft he nam hyo twelfe & 
on-gan heom seggen þa þing þe heom to-wearde 
wæren. 

þt we nu astigeð to ierusalem. & mannes sune 
beoð ge-seald sacerde ealdren & boceren. & 
ealdren & hyo hine deaðe ge-nyþerieð. & hyo 
hine þeoden sylleð. 

& hine bysemeriad. & hyo hym on spæteð. & hine 
swingeð. & of-sleað hine. & he arist on þam 
þridðen daige. 

Him þa ge-neahlahten to Iacobus & Iohannes 
zebedeus sunu. & cwæðen. Lareow we willeð þt 
þu us do swa hwæt swa we byddað. 

Þa cwæð he hwæt wille gyt þt ic inc do. 

Þa cwæðen hyo. Syle unc þt wit sitten on 
þinen wuldre. an on þinen swiðren healfe. & 
oder on þinen winstren. 

Ða cwæð se hælend. gyt nyten hwæt gyt 
byddað. Mage gyt drincen þanne calix þe ic 
drinke. & beon ge-fulled on þam fulluhte þe ic 
beo ge-fullod. 

Ða cwæðen hyo wit magen. Þa cwæð se hælend. 
gyt drincað þanne calicx. þe ich drince. gyt 
beoð ge-fullod þa fulluhte þe ic beo ge-fullod. 

Soðlice nis hit na min inc to sylle þæt gyt 
sitten on mine swiðren healfe. odðe on þa 
wynstren. ac þam þe hit ge-gearewod is. 

Þa ge-bulge þa teone hyo be Iacobe & johanne. 

Ða cleopede se hælend hyo & cwæð. Wite ge þt 
þa þe on þeoden ealderscype hæbbeð þæt 
heore ealdres anweald ofer hyo hæbbeð. 

Soðlice on eow hit nis swa. ac swa hwilc swa wile 
mid eow eldest beon. se beoð eower þen. 

& se on eow wile fermest beon. se beoð ealre 
þeow. 

Soðlice ne com mannes sune. þæt him man 
þenode. ac þt he þenode. & his sawle sealde for 
manegre alysendnysse. 

Ða comen hyo to jerico. & he ferde fram ierico & 
his leorning-cnihtes & micel manege & timeus sunu 
bartimeus sunu sæt blind wið þanne weig wædle. 

þa he ge-herde þt hit wæs se nazareisca 
hælend. he on-gan clepien. & cwæðen. Hælend 
dauiðes sune ge-miltse me. 

Þa buden him manege þæt he swigeden. he 
cleopede þa þæs þe ma. miltse me dauiðes 
sune. 

Ða æt-stod se hælend & het hine clepian. Ða 
saigden hyo þam blinden. beo ge-heortra & aris. 
se hælend þe clypað. 

he þa his reaf awarp. & forð ræsde. & to him 
com. 

Ða cwæð se hælend. hwæt wilt þu þæt ic þe 
do. þa cwæð he. lareow. þt ic ge-seo. 

þa cwæð se hælend to him. Ga; þin ge-leafe. 
þe halne ge-dyde. & he sona ge-seah. & hym felgde 
on weige. 

Þa he ge-nehlahte ierusalem & bethania to oliuete 
dune. he sende his twegen leorning-cnihtes. 

& cw. to heom. Fareð to þam castele þe on-gean 
inc ys & gyt þær sone ge-meteð assen fole 
ge-teidne; ofer þane nan man geot ne sæt. 
unteigeð hine & to me ge-lædeð. 

And gyf hwa to ginc aht cweð; seggeð þt drihten 
hæfd his neode. & hyo hine sona hider læt. 

& þa hyo ut ferden hyo ge-metten þanne fole ut 
on twi-cinan be-foran dure ge-teigdne. þa 
unteigden hyo hine. 

& sume þe þær stoden þus saigden heom. Hwat do 
gyt þan folen unteygende. 

þa cwæðen hyo swa se hælend unc bead. & hyo 
leten hyo þa. 

Ða lædden hyo þanne folan to þam hælende. & 
hyo heora reaf on aleigden. & he on sæt. 

Manega heore reaf on þane weig strehten. sume þa 
boges of þam trewen heowan. & streoweden on 
þanne weig. 

& þa þe be-foren eoden & þa þe æfter folgeden 
cwæðen þus. osanna; syo ge-bletsed se þe com 
on drihtenes name. 

sy bletsed þæt rice þe com ures fæder dauiðes 
osanna on hehnyssen. 

& he eode þa on ierosolima temple. & ealle þing 
he be-sceawede. Ða afen time wæs he ferde to 
bethania mid his twelf leorning-cnihten. 

And oþren daige þa hyo ferden fram bethanie him 
hingrede. 

Ða he ferren ge-seah an fic-treow þe leaf 
hæfde. he com & sohte hwæðer he þær on aht 
funde. þa he him to com; ne funde he þær buton 
leaf ane. Sodlice hit wæs þas fic-treowes time. 

Ða cwæð he. heonen forð on ecnysse ne æte 
anig man wæstme of þe. & his leorning-cnihtes 
þt ge-hyrden. 

Ða comen hyo eft to ierusalem & þa he on þt 
tempel eode. he gan drifen of þam tempel syllende 
& byggende. & munetera þrocu. & heah-setle. þe 
þa culfran cheptan he to-bræc. 

& he ne ge-þafode þt anig man anig fet þurh þa 
tempel bære 

& he þa lærende þus cwæð to heom. Nis his 
awriten þt min hus fram eallen þeoden beoð 
ge-nemned bed hus. soðlice ge dyden þt to 
scaþene scerefe. 

Ða þare sacerde ealdres & þa boceres þis 
ge-hyrden. hyo þohten hu hyo hine for-spilden. 
þeah hyo heom on-drædden hine. for þan eall syo 
manigeo wundrede be his lære. 

& þa hit æfen wæs he eode of þare ceastre. 

On morgen þa hyo ferden. hyo ge-seagen þt 
fic-treow for-scruncen of þam wert-rumen. 

Ða cw. petrus. Lareow. loca hu for-scranc þt 
fic-treo þe þu wergedest. 

þa cwæð se hælend him andsweriende. hæbbed 
godes truwan 

ic segge eow to soðe. swa hwilc swa cwæð to 
þise munte. syo þu aferred & on sæ aworpen. & 
on his heorte ne tweoneð ac ge-lyfð swa hwæt 
swa he cweð ge-wurðe þis. hit ge-wurð. 

for þan ic eow segge swa hwæt swa ge gyrnende 
bydðed ge-lyfað þt ge hit on-foð & hit eow 
be-cymð. 

And þanne ge standed eow to ge-byddenne. 
for-gyfeð gyf ge hwæt agen anigene hæbbeð. 
þæt eow eower senne for-gieue. eower hefenlice 
fæder se þe on heofene ys. 

Gyf ge þanne ne for-gyfeð. ne eow eower senne ne 
for-gyfð ower heofenlice fæder. 

Þa com he eft to Ierusalem. & þa he on þam 
temple eode him to ge-neahlacten þa 
heah-sacerdes. & boceres & ealdres. 

& þus cwæðen. On hwilcen anwealde dest þu þas 
þing. & hwa sealde þe þisne anweald þt þu 
þis do. 

Þa cwæð se hælend. & ic axie eow anre spræce 
andsweriað me. & ic segge eow þanne on hwilcen 
an-wealde ic þis do. 

Hwæðer wæs iohannes fulluht þe of heofene þe 
of mannen andsweried me. 

Ða þohten hyo & cwæðen be-tweoxe heom. gyf we 
seggeð of heofene. he segð us hwi ne ge-lyfde ge 
hym. 

gyf we seggeð of mannen. we on-drædeð þis 
folc. ealle hyo hafden Iohannem þt he wære 
soðlice witege. 

Ða andswereden hyo þam hælende & cwæðen. we 
nyten. Þa cwæð se hælend ne ic eow ne segge on 
hwilcen anwealde ic þas þing do. 

Þa on-gan he heom bispell seggen. Summan hym 
plantede wingeard. & be-tynde hine. & dealf ænne 
seað & tymbrede ænne stepel. & ge-sytte hine mid 
eorð-tilian. & ferde on æðelðeodinysse. 

Ða sende he to þam tiligen his þeow on tide. 
þt he þas wingeardes wæstme on-fenge. 

þa swungen hyo þane & for-leten hine ydel-hende. 

And eft he heom sende oðerne þeow. & hyo þane 
on heafde ge-wundeden. & mid teonen ge-swencten. 

Ænd eft he heom sumne sende & hy þane of-slogen. 
& manege oðre. sume hyo beoten. sume hyo 
of-slogen. 

Þa hæfde he þa gyt ænne leofestne sune. þa 
sende he æt þam nexten heom þane. & cwæð. 
Witodlice mine sune hyo for-wandigeð. 

Ða cwæðen þa tilien. heom be-tweonen. Her is 
se earfednume uton of-slean hine. þanne beoð ure 
syo earfweardnys. 

Hyo þa of-slogen hine. & wurpen wið-ute þanne 
wingeard. 

hwæt deð þas wingeardes hlaford. he cymð & 
for-deð þa tiligen. & sylð oþren þanne 
wingeard. 

Ne redde ge þis ge-writ. Se stan þe þa werhten 
awurpen þes is ge-worðen on þare herne heafed. 

þis is fram drihten ge-worðen. & hyt is 
wunderlic on uren eagen. 

Þa smægdon hyo þt hy ge-fengen hine. & hyo 
on-drædden þa manige hyo on-cneowen þa þt he 
þis bispell be heom saigde. hyo ferden þa & hine 
for-leten. 

Ða sænden hyo to him sume of fariseum & 
herodianum. þt hyo be-fengen hine on his worden. 

Ða comen hyo & þus mid facne cwæðen. Lareow we 
witen þt þu ert sodfæst & þu ne recst be 
anigen men. ne be-sceawest þu manne ansiene. ac 
þu godes weig lærst. on sodfæstnesse. Alyfð 
gafol syllen þan caisere 

hwæðer þe we ne syllað. Þa cwæð he & heora 
lotwrences wyste. hwi fandige min. bringeð me 
þanne panig þt ich hine ge-seo. 

þa brohten hyo him. Þa saigde he heom. hwæt is 
þeos anlycnyss. & þis ge-writ. Hy cwæðen þas 
caiseres. 

Ða cwæð se hælend to heom. Agyfeð þam 
caisere þa þing þe þas caiseres synde. & gode 
þe godes synde. þa wundredon hyo be þam. 

Þa comen hym to saducej. þa saiggoð þt æriste 
ne syo. & hyo axoden. & þus cwæðen. 

Lareow moyses us wrat. Gyf hwæs broðer dead 
byoð. & leafð his wif & næfð nan bearn. þt 
hys broðer nyme his wif. & his broðer sæd 
wecce. 

Eornestlice seofe broðre wæren & se areste þa 
nam wif & warð dead. ne læfden sæde. 

þa nam se oðer hyo & warð dead. ne se sæd ne 
læfde. Ge-lice se ðridðe. 

& ealle seofene hyo hæfden & sæd ne læfden. 
Ealre eftemesta þa forð-ferde þt wif. 

On þam æriste hwilces þare seofene bið þt 
wif. hyo ealle hyo hæfden. 

Þa andswerede heom se hælend hu ne dweleged ge. 
for þan þe ge nyten þa halgen ge-write ne godes 
mægen. 

Soðlice þanne hyo of deaðe ariseð ne wifieð 
hyo ne ne yftigeð ac hyo synde swilce godes 
ængles on heofenen. 

Be þam deaðen þæt hyo arised ne ræde ge on 
moyseses boc. hu god to heom cwæð. ofer þanne 
gorst-beam. Ic eom abrahames god. & ysaces god. & 
Iacobes god. 

nis god deadre. ac he is libbendra soðlice swiðe 
ge dwelieð. 

Þa ge-nehlahte him an of þam bokeren þe 
ge-herde hyo smegende. & ge-seah þt he heom wel 
andswerede. & acxode hine hwæt wære ealre 
be-bode mæst. 

Þa andswerede he hym. þt is þt mæste be-bod 
ealre israele ge-herie urne drihten god. he is an 
god. 

& lufe þinne drihten god. of ælre þinre 
heorten. & of ealre þinre sawle. & eallen þinen 
mode. & of eallen þinen maigne. þt is þt 
fermeste be-bod. 

Soðlice is oðer þisen ge-lic. lufe þinne 
nexten swa þe sylfne. nis oðer mare be-bod. 

Ða cwæð se bokere. lareow wel þu on soðe 
cwæðe. þæt an god is & nis oðer buten him. 

& þt he si ge-lufod of eallen heorten. & of 
eallen andgytte. & of ealre sawle. & of ealre 
strencðe. & lufian his nextan swa hine sylfne. 
þt is mare eallen on-sægdnyssen & offrungen. 

Þa se hælend ge-seah þt he hym wislice 
andswerede he saigde hym ne ert þu feor fram 
godes rice. & hine ne dorste nan man axian. 

þa cwæð se hælend on þam temple lærende. hu 
seggeð þa boceres þt crist sy dauiðes sune. 

Dauid self cwæð to þam halgen gaste. Drihten 
cwæð to minen drihtene site on minen swidren 
healfe. odðe ic þine feond asette to fot-scamele 
þinre fote. 

Dauid self nemde hine drihten. & hwanen is he his 
sunu. & micel menige hine lufelice ge-herde. 

Ða sæde he heom on his lare. Warnieð fram 
boceren. þa willeð on ge-gyrtlen gan & beon on 
stræte ge-grette. 

& on fermesten lareow-setlen sitten on 
ge-samnungen. & þa fyrmesten setlen on 
beorscipen. 

þa þe wudewena hus for-swelged mid heora 
langsumen ge-bedan. Þa on-foð længestne dom. 

Ða sæt se hælend on-gean þane tol-scamel. & 
ge-seah hu þt folc hire feoh torfede on þane 
tol-scamel. & manige weliga torfeden fela. 

ða com an earm wudewe and warp twege feorþinges. 

Ða cleopede he his leorning-cnihtes & saide heom. 
Soðlice ic eow segge þæt þeos earme wudewe 
ealre mest brohte þare þe on þanne toll-scamel 
brohte. 

Ealle senden of þan þe hyo ge-noh hæfden. 
Soðlice þeos of hire ermðe eall þæt hyo 
hæfde sealde ealle hire and-lyfene. 

Þa he of þam temple eode. þa cw. an of his 
leorning-cnihten to him. Lareow loca hwilce stanes 
her synt. & hwilce ge-tymbrenge. þisses temples. 

þa cwæð se hælend. ne ge-seo ge ealle þas 
mycelen ge-tymbrenge. ne beoð her læfd stan ofer 
stan þe ne wurð to-worpen. 

Ða hyo sæten on oliuetes dune. on-gean þæt 
tempel. synderlice hine petrus. & Iacobus. & 
Iohannes. & Andreas acsoden. 

Sege us hwænne þas þing ge-wurðen. & hwilc 
taken beoð þanne ealle þas þing ge-wurðe 
sculen. & hwilc tacen byð þanne ealle þas þing 
on-ginneð. & beon sculen ge-ended. 

þa on-gan se hælend heom andsweriende to 
cweðen. warnieð þt eow nan man ne be-swice. 

Soðlice manege cumeð on minen namen. & cweðað. 
ic eom crist. & be-swiced manege. 

& þanne ge ge-hereð ge-fehte & ge-fyhte hlisan. 
ne on-dræde ge eow. hit byred þæt hit ge-limpe. 
ac þanne gyt nys ænde. 

Soðlice þeod arist on-gean þeode. & rice on-gen 
rice. & byoð eorðen steriunge geond stowe & 
hunger. þis synde sare angin. 

Warnieð eow sylfe. hyo sylleð eow on ge-þeohte 
& swinged on ge-samnungen. & ge standeð be-foren 
demen & kyningen for minen naman heom on 
ge-witnysse & on ealle þeode. 

Ærest ge-byreð beon þæt godspell ge-boded. 

& þanne hyo syllende eow lædeð ne for-smeage ge 
hwæt ge spræcen. ac spreceð þæt eow on þare 
tide ge-seald byð. Ne sende ge na sprecende ac se 
halge gast. 

Soðlice se broðer þanne broðer to deaðe 
sylð. & se fæder his sune. & þa bearn ariseð 
agen heore maiges. & mid deaðe hyo ge-weccæð. 

& ge beoð eallen on hatigunge for minen namen. 
Soðlice se beoð hal se þe oð ende 
þurh-wunieð. 

Þanne ge ge-seoð þare to-wardnysse asceonunge 
standen þær hyo ne scel þanne on-gyte se þe 
ræt. fleon þanne on muntes þa þe synde on 
iudéé. 

& se þe is ofer þecene ne stige he on his hus. 
ne he in ne ga þt he aht on his huse nyme. 

& se ðe byð on acere ne cherre he on-gean þt he 
his reaf nime. 

Wa kennenden on þam dagen 

byddeð þt þis on wintre ne ge-wurðe. 

Soðlice on þam dagen beoð swilce 
ge-drefednysse. swilce ge ne (sic) wurðon. of 
fremðe. þare ge sceafte þe god ge-scop. odðe 
nu. ne nane ne ge-wurdeð. 

Ænd gyf drihten þas dages ne ge-scyrte. nan 
flæsc ne wurðe hal ac for þam ge-corenen þe he 
ge-cheas he scyrte þa dages. 

Ænd gyf eow hwilc saigð witodlice her is crist. 
witodlice þær he is. ne ge-lyfe ge. 

Soðlice lease cristes & lease witegen ariseð & 
wirceð for-beacne to be-swicene. Eac gyf hit beon 
maig þa ge-corene. 

Warnied eow. nu ealle þing þe ic eow fore-sæde. 

ac on þam dagen æfter þare ge-swæncednysse 
beoð sunne aþeostred. & se mone his brihtnysse 
ne sylð. 

& heofenes steorren beoð fallende. & beoð 
astyrede þa manege þe on heofena synde. 

Ðanne ge-syeð hyo mannes suna cumende on 
ge-nipum mid mycelen maigne & wuldre. 

þanne sent he his ængles. & hyo gaderieð his 
ge-corene of feower winden of eorden heahnysse oð 
heofenes heahnysse. 

Leorniað an byspell be þam fic-treowe. þanne 
his twi beoð mare. & leaf beoð akenned. ge witen 
þæt sumer is ge-hende. 

& wite ge þanne ge þas þing ge-seoð þæt he 
ys dure ge-hende. 

Soðlice ic eow segge þt þeos cneores ne ge-wit 
ær þan ealle þas þing ge-wurðen. 

heofene & eorðe ge-witoð. witodlice mine word ne 
ge-witeð. 

Be þam daige & þare tide nan man nat. ne engles 
on heofene ne mannes sunu buton fæder ane. 

Warnied & wacieð & ge-byddað eow ge nyten 
hwænne sye tid is. 

Swa se man þe ælþeodilice ferde. for-let his 
hus. & sealde his þeowen þane an-weald 
ge-hwilces weorces. & beode þam dureworde þt he 
wacie. 

Eornestlice wacieð. ge nyten hwænne þas huses 
hlaford cymd. þe on æfen þe on midre nihte. þe 
on hancrede. þe on morgen. 

þe læs þe he eow slæpende ge-finde þanne he 
færenge cymð. 

Soðlice þt ic eow segge. eallen ic hit segge 
wakieð. 

Soðlice þa æfter twam dagen wæren eastren. & 
þa sohten þa heah-sacerdes & þa boceres hu hyo 
hine mid facne namen & of-slogen. 

Þa cwæðen hy næs na on freols-daige þy læs 
þas folces ge-hlyd wurðe. 

and þa se hælend wæs on bethania on symones 
huse anes hreofelen & þær sæt. Þa com an wif & 
hæfde hire sealfe-box deorewurðe nardes. & 
to-brokene sealf-boxe ofer his heafed aget. 

Sume hit unwurdlice for-bæren. & be-tweoxe heom 
sylfen cwæðen. for hwi wæs þises sealfe 
for-spillednyss ge-worðen. 

þeos sealfe mihte beon ge-seald to þrem hund 
panegen. & beon þearfen ge-seald & yrseden agen 
hy. 

Þa cw. se hælend. Læted hyo hwi synde ge hire 
grame. god werc hyo on me worhte. 

Soðlice symble ge hæbbed þearfen mid eow. & 
þanne ge willeð ge magen heom tæle don. me ge 
symble næbbeð. 

þeos sealde þt hyo hæfde. hyo com to smeriene 
minne lichame on berigenne. 

Soðlice ich eow segge swa hwær swa þis godspell 
ge-boded byo on eallen midden-earde byð ge-boded 
þt hyo þis on his ge-minde dyde. 

Ða iudas scarioth þt is wiðersace an of þam 
twelfen ferde to þam heah-sacerden þt he hine 
heom be-leawde. 

Ða hyo þis ge-herden hyo fageneden & be-heton 
him feoh to syllene. & he smaigde hu he hine 
digelice sealde. 

And þam formen daige azimorum. þa hyo eastren 
offredon. his leorning-cnihtes him saiden hwider 
wilt þu þt we faren. & ge-gærewian þe þt þu 
eastren æte. 

Þa sende he twegen of his leorning-cnihten & 
sæden heom. Gað on þas cestre & ginc ágen 
yrnð sum man berende sume wæter-flaxan. Folgieð 
him. 

& swa hwider swa he ingað segged þas huses 
hlaferde. Ure lareow sægð hwær is min gyst-hus 
& min ge-reord. hwær æte ic eastren mid minen 
leorning-cnihten. 

And he inc ge-swuteleð micele halle ge-þefte. & 
ge-gerewiað us þare. 

þa ferden his leorning-cnihtes & comen on þare 
cestre & funden hit eall swa he saigde. & 
ge-garewedon þa eastren. 

Soðlice þa æfen com heom twelf mid him. 

sittende. & etende sæde se hælend. Soðlice ic 
eow segge. þt eower an þe mid me æt ge-syld me. 

þa ongunnen hio beo dreorige. & be-twuxe heom 
cwæðen. cwedst þu eom ic hit. 

Ða sæde he heom. an of eow twelfen me sylð. Se 
þe his hand on disce mid me dypd. 

Ænd witodlice mannes sune gað swa be hym awriten 
is. Wa þam men þurh þane þe mannes sune beoð 
ge-seald. betere hym wære þt se man akenned 
nære. 

Heom þa ætende afeng se hælend hlaf. & hine 
bletsiende bræc. & sealde heom & þus cwæð. 
nymed þis is min lichame. 

& onfeng calice & gode þances dyde. & sealde 
heom. & ealle heon ofdruncen. 

Ða saide he heom þis is min blod þare nywe 
cyðnissan. þt beoð for manigen agoten. 

Soðlice ic eow segge þt ic henen forð ne drince 
of þises win-geardes kynne. oððe þanne daig 
þanne ic hine neowe drince on godes rice. 

Ænd ge-cweðenen lofe hyo ferdon on ele-bergene 
munt. 

Þa cw se hælend ealle ge beoð ge-untreowsede on 
þisse nihte. for þam þe hit awriten is. ic slea 
þanne heorde. & beoð þa scep to-dræfde. 

Ac æfter þan þe ic arise ic cume be-foren eow. 
on galilea. 

Þa saide petrus him. þeah þe ealle swician. ne 
swicige ic þe ná. 

Ða cwæð se hælend. Soðlice ic þe segge. þt 
þu on þisen nihte ær coc twewe cræwe þreowe 
wið-sæcst min. 

& he þæs þe mare spæc. & þah me ge-berige mid 
þe to sweltene. ne æt-sace ic þin. & swa hyo 
cwæðen ealle. 

Ða comen hyo to anen tune þas nama wæs 
getsemani. & he cwæð to his leorning-cnihten. 
Sitteð her oð þt ic me ge-bidde. 

& he nam þa mid him petrum & iacobum. & iohannem 
þa on-gan he forhtigen & sarigen. 

& sæde heom. Vnrot is min sawle odðe deað 
ge-biddeð her & wakieð. 

Ða he lithwon forð-stop. he astrehte hine ofer 
þa eorðan & ge-bæd. gyf hit beon mihte. þt he 
on þare tide fram him ge-wite. 

& þa cw. he. abba. þt is fader on ure ge-þeode 
alle þing þe sende mihtilice afyrre þisne calic 
fram me. ac na þt ic wille ác þt þu. 

Ða com he & funde hyo slæpende. & cwæð to 
petre. Simon slæpst þu. ne mihtest þu ane tide 
wacien. 

wacieð & ge-biddað þt ge on costnunge ne gan. 
witodlice se gast is geare. ac þt flæsc is 
untrum. 

And eft he ge-bæd þa ylcen spæce. 

& þa he hine eft agen be-wende. he funde hyo 
slæpende. heore eagen wæren ge-hefegede. & hyo 
nyston hwæt hyo him andswereden. 

Þa com he ðriddan siðe. & sæde heom slæpeð 
nu & resteð ge-noh hit is. time is cumen nu is 
mannes sune ge-seald on synfulre hande. 

arised uten gan. nu is ge-hende se þe me syld. 

him þa þe gyt spræcende com iudas scarioth þt 
is wiðer-saca. an of þam twelfen. & mid him 
mycel manige. mid sweorden & mid sahlen. fram 
heah-sacerden & bokeren & ealdren. 

Soðlice his læwa heom taken sealde & þus 
cwæð. Swa hwilcne swa ic kysse. se hit ys nymeð 
& lædeð hine wærlice. 

& sone swa he com he ge-nehlacte hine to & cwæð. 
Lareow; & cyste hine. 

& hyo heore hande on hine wurpen & namen hine. 

Soðlice an of þam þe þær embe-uten stoden his 
sweord abræd. & slog þas sacerdes þeow. & his 
eare of acarf. 

Ða cwæð se hælend heom and-sweriende. Swa swa 
to anen scæðan ge ferden mid sweorden & treowen 
me ge-fon. 

þanne ic daig-hwamlice mid eow wæs on temple 
lærende & ge me namen. ac þt þa ge-write syen 
ge-fellde. 

Ða for-leten his leorning cnihtes ealle hine & 
flugen. 

Sum gungling him fylgde mid ane scytan be-wæfed 
nacod. & hy name hine. 

þt wærpendre þare scete nacod he heom fram 
fleah. 

& hy lædden þanne hælend to þam heah-sacerde 
ænd comen ealle þa sacerdes. ænd bokeres. & 
ealdres. to-gædere. 

Petrus heom felgede ferren oð þas heah-sacerdes 
cæfertun. and he set mid þam þenum & wermden 
hine æt þam fyre. 

Ða heah-sacerdas sohten & eall ge-þeaht. tale 
agen þanne hælend. þt hyo hine to deaðe 
sealden & hyo ne fundon. 

Manege sæden lease cyðnyssen agen hine. & þa 
cyðnisse næren þas-lice. 

Ða arise sume & saigden lease cydnysse agen hine 
& þus cwæðen. 

Sodes we ge-hyrden hine seggen ic to-weorpe þis 
hand-worhte temple. & æfter þrem dagen ic oðer 
un-hand-worht ge-timbrige. 

& heore cydnysse næs þas-gelic. 

Ða aras sum heah-sacerd on heora midlene & acxode 
þanne hælend. Ne andswerest þu nan þing agen 
þt þas þe onweorped. 

he swegede & naht ne andswerede. Eft hine axode se 
heah-sacerd. Ert þu crist. Þas ge-bletsedes 
godes sune. 

Þa sæde se hælend ic eom. & ge ge-seoð mannes 
sune on swiðren healfe sitten. his maignes. & 
cumende mid heofenes ge-nipen. 

Ða cwæð se heah-sacerd his reaf slytende. hwi 
wilnige we gyt cyðera. 

ge ge-herden his bismer. hwæt þincð eow. Ða 
hyrden hyo ealle hine & cwæðen. þt he wære 
deaðes scyldig. 

Ænd sume agunnen hym on spæten. & ofer-wreon his 
ansiene. & mid festen hine beaten. & him to 
cwæðen. Ared. & þa þenas hine mid handen 
beoten. 

& þa petrus wæs on cæfertune þa com to him an 
þinen þas heah-sacerdes. 

& þa hye ge-seah petrum wermende þa cwæð hy. 
Þu wære mid þam nazareiscen hælende. 

Ða æt-soc he & cwæð. Ic nat ne ic kan hwæt 
þu saigst. & he eode þa of þam cæfertune & se 
coc creow. 

Eft þa hine cneow oðer þinen. & hyo on-gan 
cweðen to þam þe þær abuten stoden. Soðlice 
þes is of þam. 

& he eft æt-soc. Ænd eft þa embe litel þa þe 
eft stoden cwæðen to petre. Soðlice þu ert of 
þam galileisc þu ert. 

Ða æt-gan he of-sacan. & swerien. soðes ne can 
ic þanne man þe ge seggeð. 

& þa eft sone creow se coc. Ða ge-munde petrus 
þas hælendes word þe he him saide. ær se coc 
creowe twige. þrewe þu me æt-sæcst. þa on-gan 
he wepen. 

Ða sone on morgen worhten þa heah-sacerdes heore 
ge-mot. mid ealdren & boceren. & eallen werede & 
lædden þane halend ge-bunden & sealden hine 
pilaten. 

Ða axode pilatus hine eart þu iudea kining. Ða 
andswerede he hym. Ðu hit sægst. 

Þa wreiden hine þa heah-sacerdes. on manegen 
þingen. 

Eft pilatus hine axode ne andswerest þu nan 
þing. loca hu mycelen hyo þe wreigeð. 

Ða ne andswerede se hælend him nam mare swa 
þæt pilatus wundrede. 

On sym-mel-daig wæs his ge-wune. þt he heom 
for-gefe ænne bundenne swa hwilcne swa hyo 
bæden. 

Ða bæden hyo barraban. se wæs ge-bunden mid 
þam replingen. se þurh swice-cræft man-slyht 
worhten. 

& þa he ferde þa on-gan syo manigeo hine biddan 
swa hy symle dyden. 

Ða cwæð pilatus. Wille ge þt ic eow for-gefe 
iudea kyning. 

he wiste þt þurh ande hine sealden þa 
heah-sacerdas. 

Ða astireden þa biscoppes þa manige þt he heom 
barraban for-gefe. 

Eft pilatus him andswerede. hwæt do ic be iudea 
kyninge. 

hyo eft grætten & cwæðen. hoh hine. 

Þa saigde pilatus. hwæt yfeles dyde he. hyo þas 
þe ma cleopeden ahoh hine. 

Pilatus wolde þa þam folce ge-cwemen. & for-gef 
heom barraban. & sealde heom þanne hælend 
be-swungen þt he ahangen wære. 

Þa lædden þa cempen hine on þas domernes 
cæfertun & hyo to-gædere ealle wered cleopeden. 

& scridden hine mid purpren & him on setten 
þernene helm awundene. 

& on-gunnen hine þus greten. hal beo þu iudea 
kyning. 

& beoton hine on þt heafeð mid reode & spetten 
him on & hire cneow beigden & hine ædmetten. 

Ænd syððen hyo hine bismeredon. un-scriddan 
hine þam purpran. & scriddan hine mid his reafen. 
& lædden hine þæt hyo hine ahengen. 

& ge-nedden sumne weig-ferende symonem cyreneum 
cumende of þam tune alisandres fader & ruffi. þt 
he his rode bære. 

& hyo lædden hine on þam stowe golgotha. þt is 
on ure þeode ge-reht heafed-panna stowa. 

& sealden him ge-bytered win & he hit ne on-feng. 

And þa hyo hine ahengen hyo dælden his reaf & 
hlote wurpen. hwæt ge-hwa name. 

Ða wæs under-tid. & hyo ahengen hine. 

& ofer-ge-writ his geltes wæs awriten iudea kyng. 

& hyo ahengen mid him twegen scaðen ænne on his 
swiðeren healfe. & oðerne on his winstren. 

þa wæs þt ge-writ ge-fylled þt cwæð. & he 
wæs mid unriht-wisan ge-teald. 

And þa þe forð-stopen hine gremedon & hyra 
heafod cwehten. & þus cwæðen. Wala se to-werpð 
þt tempel. & on ðrim dagen eft ge-tymbred. 

ge-hæl þe sylfne of þare rode stigende. 

Eal swa þa heah-sacerdas bysmeriende be-twexe 
þam bokeren cwæðen. odre he hæle ge-dyde. hine 
sylfne he ne maig halne don. 

Crist israele kyng astig nu of rode þt we ge-seon 
& ge-lefen. And þa þe mid him ahangeden wæren 
him mid ge-bundene. 

And þare syxte tide wurðe þeostre ge-worðene 
geond ealle eorðan. odðe non-tide. 

And to non-tide se hælend clepede mycele stefne 
heloy heloy lama sabathani. þt is on ure 
ge-þeode. min god min god. hwi for-lædst þu me. 

& sume þe þær abuton stoden & þis ge-hyrdon 
hyo cwæðen. nu þes clyped heliam. 

þa arn hyre an. & fylde ane spunge mid eisile. & 
on reod sette & him drincen sealde. & cwæð. 
læteð þt we ge-seon hwæðer helias cume hine 
niðer to settenne. 

Se hælend þa asende his stefne & forð-ferde. 

Ænd þas temples wah-irift wæs to-sliten on twa 
of ufewearden odðe niðeweard. 

Ða þas hundredes man þe þær stod agen ge-seah 
þt se hælend swa clepiende forð-ferde. he 
cwæð. Soðlice þes man wæs godes sune. 

And þa wif wæren feorren be-healdende. & betwux 
þam wæs sie magdalenisce Marie. & Marie iacobes 
moðer & saloméé. 

& þa he wæs on galiléé hy felgden hym. & him 
þenoden & manege oðre þe him mide ferden on 
ierusalem. 

Ænd þa æfen wæs ge-worden þt wæs parasceue. 
þt is ær sæterdaige 

þa com iosep se æðele refe of arimathia se 
sylfe godes rice ge-an-bidode. & he dyrstilice in 
to pilate eode & bæd þas hælendes lichame. 

Þa wundrede pilatus gyf he þa gyt forð-ferde. 
Ða clypede he þanne hundredes man. & hine axode 
hwæðer he dead wære. 

Ða he wiste þt. þa agyf he þane lic-hame 
iosepe. 

Ða bohte iosep ane scytan & hine þær-on 
be-feold & on byrigenne leigde syo wæs of stane 
aheawan. & wyltel ænne stan to þare berienne 
dure. 

Þa com Marie magdalene & Iosepes Marie. & 
be-heolden hwær he ge-leigd wære. 

& þa saternes daig wæs agan sye magdalenisce 
Marie & Iacobes Marie & saloméé bohten 
wert-ge-mang þt hyo comen & hine smereden. 

Ænd swiðe ær anen reste-daige comen to þare 
byregenne up asprungenne sunna. 

& cwæðen heom be-tweonen. hwa awylt us þysne 
stan of þare byregene dure. 

Þa hyo hy be-seagen. hyo ge-seagen þane stan 
aweig aweldne. soðlice he wæs swiðe mycel. 

Ænd þa hyo eoden on þa byregenne hyo ge-seagen 
ænne geongne on þam swiðren healfe sittende 
hwiten gerlen ofer-wrogene. & hyo þa forhteden. 

Þa cw he to heom ne fortige ge na. ge seceð 
þane nazarenisca hælend ahangene. he aras. nis 
he her. her is syo stowe þær hy hine leigden. 

ac fareð & seggeð his leorning-cnihten. & petre. 
þt he gæd to-foren eow on galilee. Þær ge hine 
ge-seoð swa he eow sæde. 

& hyo ut eoden & flugen fram þare byrigene. & 
wæren aferde. for þare sihðe þe hyo ge-seagen. 
& hyo nane men naht ne saigden. soðlice hyo heom 
an-dredden. 

Þa he aras on ærne morgen on reste-daige; ærest 
he atewde þare magdalenisca marie of þare þe he 
ut adraf seofen deofel-seocnysse. 

& hy þa ut eode & hit þam cydde þe mid him 
wæren heofende & weopende. 

þa hyo ge-hyrden þt he leofede & hyo hine 
ge-seagen. þa ne lyfden hyo him. 

Æfter þam heom twam he wæs atewed on oðren 
heowe. heom on þane tun farende. 

& hyo þa foran. & þt odren cydden. & hye heom ne 
ge-lyfden. 

Ða æt þan ytemesten hyo ænd-lefene æt mete 
sæten. heom atewede se hælend & here unbelefen & 
heora heorten ge-tremede. for-þan þt hye hine 
ge-seagen arise hi hit ne ge-lyfden. 

& he saide heom. Gað swa wid swa midden-eard 
bodiende þt godspel ealle ge-scefte. 

þt se þe ge-lyfd & is ge-funted he is hal. & ge 
se þe ne ge-lyfd he is for-demd. 

Þa tacnen þe hæbbed þa þe ge-lyfeð þis 
folgeð. On mine name deofle gad ut. tungen 
spreced neowe. 

& naddren be-nemed. & gyf he deadlice drenc 
drinced ne mag he heom derigen. & gyf hye uppen 
seocen here hande asetteð þe bet heom scel 
wurðe. 

& ure hlaford hælend crist seððen he wið heom 
ge-sprecen hæfde; he astah in to heofene & sitt 
on godes swiðre. 

Hyo þa fulfelde bodeden swa wid swa al. þas 
hlafordes weorces & his bispelles fulfellende mid 
felgenden tacnen. AMEN. 

LUKE 

for þan þe witodlice manega þohte þare þinge 
race ge-ende-berden þe on us ge-fylde synde; 

swa us be-tahten þa þe hyt of fremðe ge-sægen. 
& þare spræce þéenæs wæren. 

Me ge-þuhte geornlice eallen oð ænde-byrdnysse 
writen þe þu seleste theophilus. 

þt þu oncnawe þare worde sodfæstnysse of þam 
þe þu ge-læred ært. 

On herode dagen iudea cyninges wæs sum sacerd on 
namen zacharias of abian tune. & his wif wæs of 
áárones dohtren. & hire name wæs elisabeth. 

Soðlice hyo wæren ba twa rihtwise be-foren gode. 
& gangenden on eallen hys beboden & rihtwisnesse. 
ba twa wrohte. 

& hyo nafden nan bearn. for-ðan elisabeth wæs 
un-berende & hyo on heore dagen baðe forð-eoden. 

Soðlice wæs ge-worðen þa zacharias hys 
sacerd-hades brea. on his ge-wrixles endebyrdnysse 
be-fore gode. 

æfter ge-wunan. þara sacerdes hades hlotes he 
eode þæt he his offringe sette. Ða he on godes 
tempel eode 

eall wered þas folkes wæs ute biddende on þare 
offrenge timen. 

Ða atewede hym drihtenes ængel standende on þas 
weofedes swiðren healfe. 

Þa warð zacharias ge-drefed þæt ge-seonde & 
him eige on-reas. 

Ða cwæð se ængel hym to. ne on-dred þu þe 
zacharias. for þan þin bene is ge-herd. & þin 
wif elisabeth þe sune kenð. & þu nemnest hys 
name Iohannes 

& he byð þe to blisse. & manega on his 
akynnednysse ge-fageneð. 

Soðlice he byð mære be-foren drihtene. & he ne 
drincð win ne beor. & he beoð ge-felleð mid 
halgen gaste; Þanne gyt of hys moder innoðe. 

& manege israele bearne he ge-chyrd to drihtene 
heore gode 

& he gæð to-foren him on gaste. & on helias 
ge-mihte. & he fæderan heortan to heora bearnan 
ge-cyrre. & ungeleafulle. to rihtwise gleaw-scipe. 
drihtne fulfremed folc ge-gærewian. 

Ða cwæð zacharias to þam engle. hwanan wat ich 
þis. Ic eom nu eald & min wif on heora dagen 
forð-eode. 

Þa andswerede him se ængel. Ich eom gabriel se 
engel. ic þe stande be-foren gode. & ich eom 
asend wið þe sprecen. & þe þis bodien. 

End nu abydst swigende. & þu spræken ne miht oð 
þanne dayg þe þas þing gewurðad. for þan þu 
mine worden ne lyfdest þa byð on heora timan 
ge-fylde. 

And þæt folc wæs zachariam ge-abydende. & 
wundredon. þæt he on þæt temple ge-læt wæs. 

Ða he ut-eode ne mihte he heom to spræcen. & hyo 
on-cneowen þæt he on þam temple sume ge-sihte 
ge-seah. & he wæs beacniende heom & dumb 
þurh-wunede. 

Þa wæs ge-worðen þa his þenunga dages 
ge-fylde wæren. he ferde to his huse. 

Soðlice æfter dagen elisabeth his wif 
ge-eacnode. & hy be-dyglede hyo fif monðas & 
cwæð. 

Soðlice me drihten ge-dyde þus on þam dagen þe 
he ge-seah mine hosp be-twux mannen afyrran. 

Soðlice on þam syxten monðe wæs a-send gabriel 
se engel fram drihtene on galiléé cestre þare 
name wæs nazareth. 

to be-weddedre femnen anen were þas name wæs 
ioseph of dauiðes huse. & þare femne name wæs 
mariam. 

Ða cwæð se ængel ingangende. Hal wæsse þu 
mid gyfe ge-fylled. drihten mid þe. Þu ert 
ge-bletsed on wifen. 

þa warð hyo on his spræce ge-drefed. & þohte 
hwæt syo gretunge wære. 

Ða cwæð se ængel. ne on-dræd þu þe Maria. 
Soðlice þu gyfe mid gode ge-mettest 

soðlice nu þu on innoðe ge-eacnest. & sune 
censt ænd hys name hælend ge-nemnest 

& se byoð mære. & þas heagestes sune ge-nemned. 
& hym sylð drihten god his fæder dauides setll. 

& he rixad on echnesse on Iacobes huse. & his 
riche ænde ne beoð. 

Þa cwæð maria to þam ængle hu ge-wurð þis 
for þan ich were ne on-cnawe. 

Ða andswerede hyre se ængel. Se halge gast on 
þe be-kymd & þas heagestan mihte þe 
ofer-scædeð. & for þan þt halig þe of þe 
akenned byð; byð godes sune ge-nemned. 

Ænd nu elisabeth þin mage sune on hire elde 
ge-echnede. & þes moneð is hire syxto sye is 
unberende ge-nemned. 

for-þy nis ælch word mid gode unmihte-lic. 

Ða cwæð Maria. Her is drihtenes þinen. 
ge-wurðe me æfter þinen worde. & se ængel hire 
fram ge-wat. 

Soðlice on þam dagen aras Maria & ferde on 
muntlande mid efste. on iudeisse ceastre. 

& eode in-to zacharias huse. & grette elisabeth. 

Ða wæs ge-worðen. þa helisabeth ge-herde maRie 
gretinge. þa ge-fagene þæt chyld on hire 
innoðe. ænd þa warð elisabeth halgen gaste 
ge-fylled. 

ænd hyo cleopede hludere stefne. & cwæð. Ðu 
ært be-twux wifen ge-bledsed. & ge-bletsed ys 
þines innoðes wæstme. 

& hwanen is me þis þæt mines drihtenes moder 
scolde to me cume. 

Sone swa þinre gretinge stefne on minan earen 
ge-worðan wæs. þa fagenede min chyld on minen 
innoðe. 

Ænd eadig þu ert þu þe ge-lyfdest þæt 
fulfremede sinde þa þing. þe þe fram drihtene 
ge-saigde synde. 

Ða cwæð maria min saule mersed drihten. 

and min gast ge-blissode on gode minen hælende. 

For þam þe he ge-seah his þinene eadmodnysse. 
Soðlice henen-forð me eadige seggeð ealle 
cneornesse. 

for þam þe me mychele þing dyde se þe mihtyg 
ys. & his name is halig 

& hys mildheortnysse of cneornisse. on cneornesse 
hine on-drædende. 

He worhte mægne on hys earme. he to-dælde þa 
ofermode. on moda heora heortan. 

He warp þa rice of setlle. & þa eadmode he up 
an-hof. 

Hyngriende he mid gode ge-felde. & þa ofor-mode 
ydele for-let. 

He afeng israel his cniht & ge-mynde hys 
mildheortnysse. 

Swa he spræc to ure fæderen abrahame. & his 
sæde on a weorlde. 

Soðlice Marie wunede mid hire swylce þreo 
monðes; & ge-wende þa to hire huse. 

Ða wæs afelled elisabethe kenning-tyd. & hyo 
sune kende. 

ænd hire nehcheburas & hyre cuðan þæt 
ge-herden þæt drihten hys mildheortnysse mid 
hire mærsede. & hyo mid hire blisseden. 

Þa on þam ehtode daige hyo comon þæt chyld to 
embscniðen. & nemden hine his fæder name 
zachariam. 

Þa andswerede his moder nese soðes. ac he beoð 
Iohan ge-nemned. 

Ða cwæðen hyo to hire. nis nan on þinre 
mægðe þisse name ge-nemned. 

Ða cwæðen hyo to his fæder. hwæt he wolde 
hine ge-nemned beon. 

þa wrat he ge-beðenen wexbrede Iohannes ys hys 
name. Ða wundredon hyo ealle. 

Ða warð sona hys muð & hys tunge ge-opened & he 
spræc drihten bletsiende. 

Ða warð eige ge-worden ofer ealle heora 
nehchegeburas & ofer ealle iudea munt-land wæren 
þas worð wið-mærsede. 

& ealle þa þe hyt ge-hyrdon on heore heorten 
setten & cwæðen. Wenst þu hwæt beoð þes 
cnapa; witoðlice drihtnes hand wæs mid hym. 

Ænd zacharias hys fæder wæs mid halgen gaste 
ge-fylled. & he wito-gode. & cwæð. 

Ge-bletseð syo drihten israele god; for þan þe 
he ge-neosede. & hys folces alysendnysse dyde. 

Ænd he us hæle horn arærde on dauides huse. hys 
cnihtes. 

Swa he spræc þurh hys halgene witegene muð. Ða 
þe of weorldes fremðe spræken. 

& he alesde us of uren feonden. & of ealre þare 
handen þe us hateden. 

Mildheortnysse to werchen mid ure fæderen. & 
ge-munen hys halgen kyðnesse. 

hyne us to sellene þanne að þe he uren fader 
abrahame swor. 

þæt we buton eyge of ure feondon handen alesde 
hym þeowian. 

on halignesse be-foran hym eallen ure dagen. 

& þu cnapa gæst & beost þas heageste witega 
ge-nemned. Ðu gæst be-foran drihtnes ansiene hys 
wegas gearewian. 

To syllene hys folce his halge ge-wit on hira 
synna for-gefenyssa. 

Ðurh innoðes ures godes mildheortnyssa. on þam 
he us neosede. of east-dæle up-springende. 

on-lihtan þam þe on þeostrum & on deaðes scade 
sitteð. ure fet to ge-reccenne on sibbe weig. 

Soðlice se cnape weox. & wæs on gaste 
ge-stræncþed. & wæs on westene oð þanne dayg 
his atewednysse on israel. 

Soðlice on þam dagen wæs ge-worðen ge-bod fram 
þan caisere auguste. þæt eall ymb-hwyrft wære 
to-mærcod. 

Ðeos to-mearcednysse wæs ærest ge-worðen. fram 
þan deman syrige cyrino. 

& ealle hyo eoden & syndrie ferden on heore 
ceastre. 

Ða ferde ioseph fram galilea. of þare ceastre 
nazareht. on iudeissce ceastre. dauiðes syo is 
ge-nemned bethléém. for þan þe he wæs of 
dauiðes huse & hyrde 

þæt he ferde mid marian þe hym ge-wedded wæs. 
& wæs ge-eacnod. 

Soðlice wæs ge-worðan þa hyo þær wæren. 
hyre dages wæren ge-fyllede þæt hyo kende 

& hyo þa akende hire frum-kennedan sunu. & hine 
mid cyld-claþen be-wand. & hine on binne alegde. 
for þan þe hyo næfden rum on cumene huse. 

Ænd heordas wæren on þam ylcan riche wakiende. 
& niht-wæccen healdende ofer heore heorda. 

Þa stod drihtnes ængel wið hyo & godes 
brihtnysse heom ymbe-scan; & hyo heom mychel eige 
adredden. 

& se engel heom to cwæð. Nelle ge eow 
on-dræden. soðlice nu ich eow bodige mychele 
blisse syo beoð eallen folce. 

for þan to dayg eow is hælend akenned. se is 
drihten crist on dauiðes ceastre. 

And þis taken eow beoð. Ge findað an chyld 
ræglen be-wunden. & on binne aleigð. 

And þa wæs færinge ge-worðan mid þam ængle 
myceles heofenlices weredes god heriendra. & þus 
cweðende 

gode syo wuldor on heahnysse. & on eorðan sibbe 
mannen godes willan. 

& hyt wæs ge-worðen þa þa ængles to heofene 
ferden. Þa heordan heom be-tweonen spræcen & 
cwæðen. Vton faren to bethléém. & ge-seon 
þæt word þe ge-worðen ys. þæt drihten us 
atywede. 

& hyo efstende comen & ge-metton marian & Ioseph 
ænd þæt chyld on binne aleigd. 

Ða hyo þæt ge-seagen þa on-cneowen hyo be þam 
worden þe heom ge-sæd wæs. be þam chylde. 

Ænd ealle þa þe ge-herden wundreden be þam. 
þe heom þa heordes saigdon. 

Maria ge-heold ealle þas word on hire heorte 
smeagende. 

Ða ge-wenden ham þa heordes god wuldriende. & 
heriende on eallen þan þe hyo ge-herden & 
ge-seagen. Swa to heom ge-cweðen wæs. 

Æfter þam þe ehta dages ge-felde wæren þt 
þæt chyld embsnyðen wære. Hys nama wæs 
hælend. Se wæs fram ængle ge-nemned ær he on 
innoðe ge-eacned wære. 

Æfter þam þe hire clænsing-dages ge-felde 
wæren. æfter moyses lage. hyo lædden hine on 
ierusalem þæt hyo hine gode setton 

swa swa [on] drihtnes lage awriten ys. Ðæt ælc 
wæpnyd ge-cyndlym untynende beoð drihtenes halig 
ge-nemned. 

& þæt hyo offrunge sealden. æfter þan þe 
drihtnes læge ge-cweðen is. twa turtlan. oððe 
twa culfran briddes. 

Ænd þa wæs an man on ierusalem þas name wæs 
symeon. & þes man wæs rihtwis & mid israele 
frofren ge-anbadiende. & halig gast him on wæs. 

& he andswere of þam halgen gaste on-feng. þæt 
he deað ne ge-seage buton he ær drihten crist 
ge-seage. 

Ænd on gaste he on þæt tempel com. & þa his 
mæges læddon þanne hælend. þt hyo for hym 
æfter þare læge ge-wunan dyden. 

Heo on-feng hine mid hys handen. & god bletsede. & 
cwæð. 

Drihten nu þu lætst þinne þeow æfter þine 
worde on sibbe. 

for þam mine eagen ge-seagen þine hæle. 

þa þu ge-gearwudest be-foran alre folce ansiene. 

leoht to þeoda awrigenysse. & to þines folces 
wuldre israele. 

Þa wæs hys fæder & hys moder wundriende be þam 
þe be hym ge-saigde wæren. 

And þa ge-bletsede hyo symeon. & cwæð to marian 
hys moder. loca nu þes is on hryre & on arist 
ge-sett. manegre on israele & on taken þam þe 
wið-cweðen byð. 

Ænd his sweord þine sawle þurhferð. þæt 
ge-þohtes seon awrigene of manegen heorten. 

And anna wæs witegestre fanueles dohter of 
asseres mægðe. þeos wunede manigene daig & hye 
lefede mid hire were sefe gear on hire femnehade 

& hyo wæs wudewe oð feower & hund-eahtetig 
geare. Seo of þam temple ne ge-wat daiges ne 
nihtes. þeowiende on fæstene. & on halsunge. 

And þeos þare tide be-cumende drihtne andette & 
be hym spræc. eallen þan þe ge-an-bided-en 
ierusalem alysednysse. 

& þa hyo ealle þing ge-feldon æfter drihtenes 
lage. hyo hwurfon on galiléé on hire ceastre 
nazareth. 

Soðlice þæt chyld weox & wæs gestranged 
wisdomes full. & godes geue wæs on him. 

& his mæges ferden ælche geare to ierusalem on 
eastre daiges freols-tide. 

Ða he wæs twelf wintre. hyo foren to ierusalem 
to þam easterlicen freolse. æfter hyre 
ge-wunenen (sic). 

& þa ge-fylleden dagen. þa hyo agen ge-hwurfon 
be-laf se hælend on ierusalem & hys mæges þæt 
nyston. 

wende þæt he on heore ge-ferrede wære. Ða 
comen hyo anes daiges feor. & hyo hine sohte 
be-twe oxe his mæges & hys cuðan. 

þa hyo hine ne funden; hyo ge-wenton to ierusalem 
hine sechende. 

Ða æfter þreom dagen. hyo funden hine on þam 
temple sittende. on middan þam lareowan. 
hlystende & hyo axiende. 

Ða wundredon hyo ealle þe ge-hyrden be his 
gleawscype; & his ændsweren. 

Ða cwæð his moder to him. Sune hwi dydest þu 
unc þus. þin fæder & íc sarigende þe sohten. 

Þa cwæð he to heom. hwæt is þæt gyt me 
sohten. nyste gyt þæt me ge-byred to beonne on 
þam þingen þe mines fæder synde. 

Ða ne on-geaton hyo þa word þe he to heom 
spræc. 

Ða ferde he mid heom & com to nazareth. & wæs 
heom under-þeod. And hys moder ge-heold ealle 
þas word on hire heorte smeagende. 

Ænd se hælend þeah on wisdome & on ylde. & mid 
gyfe mid gode & mid mannen. 

Soðlice þam fiftendan geare þas caiseres 
an-wealdes tyberij. be-ginnenden þam pontiscen 
pilate iudea þeode. foerðan dæles rice 
galiléé herode. philippe hys broder. feorðan 
dæles rice iturie. & þas riche traconitidis. & 
lisania abiline feorðan dæles rica. 

under þare sacerde ealdres anna & chaifa. godes 
word wæs ge-worðan ofer zacharias sune on 
westene. 

& he com into eall Iordanes riche bodiende. 
deadbote fulluht & synne for-gyfenesse 

swa hit awriten ys on ysaias bech þas witegan. 
Clepiende stefn on westene. ge-garewiað drihtenes 
weig dod his siðas rihte. 

Ælch dane beoð ge-feld. & ælch munt & beorh 
beoð ge-niðered. & þwuru beoð on ge-rihte. & 
ungerydu on smeðe weges. 

& ælc flæsc ge-sihð godes hæle. 

Soðlice he cwæð to þam mægen þe ferden þæt 
hyo wæren fullode fram hym. Eale næddrene kyn 
hwa atewedo (sic) eow þæt ge fleon fram þam 
towearde eorre. 

Doð eornestlice deadbote wæstmes. & ne on-ginnen 
ge cweðen. we hæbbed us to fader abraham. Ich 
segge eow þæt god is swa mihtig þæt he maig of 
þisen stanen abrahames bearn aweccan. 

Nu ys syo æx asett. to þas treowas wirtrumen. 
Witodlice ælch treow þe ne brincd godne wæstme 
beoð for-corfan & on fyr aworpen. 

Ða axoden hine þa manige & cwæðen; hwæt do 
we. 

Þa cwæð he to heom. se þe hafð twege tunekan. 
sylle þam þe næfð. & þam ge-lice do se þe 
metes hæfð 

Ða comen þa manfulle þæt hy aþwegene wæren. 
& cwæðen to hym lareow hwæt do we. 

Þa cwæð he ne do ge naht mare þanne þæt eow 
ge-sett ys. 

Ða axoseden (sic) hine þa cempan & cwæðen. & 
hwæt do we. Þa sæde he heom. ne sla ge nanne 
man. Ne tále ne doð. & beoð eð-healde on 
eowren andlyfenum. 

Soðlice þam folce wenenden & eallen on heore 
heorten þencenden be Iohanne hwæder he crist 
wære. 

Ða andswerede Iohannes heom eallen seggenden. 
Witodlice ic eow an watere fullige. Soðlice kymð 
strengre þanne ich; þas ich nem wurðe þæt ich 
hys scoþwang un-cnytte. Heo eow fulled on halgen 
gaste. & on fyre. 

& his fann is on his handa. & he fermed hys bernes 
flore. & gadered hys hwæte in-to hys berne. þæt 
chæf he for-bernð on un-acwenctelice fyre. 

Manega oðre þing bodiende. He þæt folc lærde. 

Herodes se feorðan dæles rica þa he wæs fram 
him ge-þread. be þare herodiscan his broder wife 
& be eallen yfelen þe herodes dyde. 

& ofer eall þæt ge-icte þæt he be-clysde 
Iohanne on cwarterne. 

Soðlice wæs ge-worðan þa eall þæt folc wæs 
ge-fullod. & þam hælende ge-fulloden & 
ge-biddenden. heofene wæs ge-opened 

& se halga gast astah lichamlicere an-syna on hine 
swa an culfre & stefne wæs of heofene ge-worðan 
& þus cwæð. Ðu ert min ge-corena sune on þe 
me ge-likeð. 

& se hælend wæs on ylde swilce þrittige wintre. 
þæt men wenden þæt he wære Iosepes sune. Se 
wæs heliges sune. 

se wæs nazareth. swa of cneornysse on cneornysse 
oððe adam. Se wæs godes sunu oð fif & 
hund-seofentig cneornisse.
